FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[CategoriesId], [c].[ProductsId], [c0].[Id], [c0].[CreatedDate], [c0].[Image], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [CategoryProduct] AS [c]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c0] ON [c].[CategoriesId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductsId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[ColorId], [p1].[CreatedDate], [p1].[ProductId], [c1].[Id] AS [Id0], [c1].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c1].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c1] ON [p1].[ColorId] = [c1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]

    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p2].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [p].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
